{"answers": ["National Industrial Recovery Act", "NIRA"], "model_answer": "The New Deal program that limited production in industry was the National Industrial Recovery Act (NIRA). NIRA was a program that aimed to stimulate economic recovery by increasing production, reducing competition, and raising prices. It was passed in 1933 and was designed to help industries recover from the Great Depression. NIRA established codes of fair competition, set minimum wages and working hours, and provided stimulus funds for public works projects. It also sought to reduce harmful competition by limiting production and promoting cooperation among industries."}

{"answers": ["prophase I of meiosis", "during prophase I of meiosis"], "model_answer": "Synapsis of homologous chromosomes does not occur in mitosis. Synapsis is a process that occurs during meiosis, specifically during prophase I, where homologous chromosomes pair up and become aligned prior to their segregation. In mitosis, chromosomes do not pair up in the same way, and instead, sister chromatids separate and move to opposite poles of the cell."}

The Articles of Confederation were a loose agreement among the 13 original states, and the government was more of a confederation of states rather than a central government.\n\nThe government under the Articles of Confederation was unable to enforce its laws"}

{"answers": ["balance sheet", "The balance sheet"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, the financial statement that involves all aspects of the accounting equation is the Balance Sheet. The Balance Sheet shows a firm's assets, liabilities, and equity (capital) at a set point in time, usually the end of the fiscal year reported on the accompanying income statement. The total assets always equal the total combined liabilities and equity in dollar amount, which demonstrates the basic accounting equation - Assets = Liabilities + Equity."}
